				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Laßt uns sorgen, laßt uns wachen, BWV 213 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>13 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1733 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Lasst uns sorgen, lasst uns wachen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Hercules auf dem Scheidewege&#160;; Hercules at the Crossroads<br />Let us take care, let us watch
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="fr, nn, en, de, nl">Laßt uns sorgen, laßt uns wachen</span>; <span title="ca">Laßt uns sorgen</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="en">Hercules at the Crossroads</span>; <span title="en">Let us take care, let us watch over</span>; <span title="de">Die Wahl des Herkules</span>; <span title="de">Hercules am Scheidewege</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/184285107">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/La%C3%9Ft_uns_sorgen,_la%C3%9Ft_uns_wachen,_BWV_213">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/184285107">184285107</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n81147595">n81147595</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300009240">300009240</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb139816340">139816340</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 213&#160;; BC G 18
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 362
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>F major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>13 movements:
<ol><li> Chorus: Laßt uns sorgen, lasst uns wachen
</li><li> Recitative (alto): Und wo? Wo ist die rechte Bahn
</li><li> Aria (soprano): Schlafe, mein Liebster, und pflege der Ruh
</li><li> Duet Recitative (soprano, tenor): Auf! folge meiner Bahn
</li><li> Aria (alto): Treues Echo dieser Orten
</li><li> Recitative (tenor): Mein hoffnungsvoller Held
</li><li> Aria (tenor): Auf meinen Flügeln sollst du schweben
</li><li> Recitative (tenor): Die weiche Wollust locket zwar
</li><li> Aria (alto): Ich will dich nicht hören
</li><li> Duet Recitative (alto, tenor): Geliebte Tugend, du allein
</li><li> Duet Aria (alto, tenor): Ich bin deine, du bist meine
</li><li> Recitative (bass): Schaut, Götter, dieses ist ein Bild
</li><li> Chorus: Lust der Volker, Lust der Deinen
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1733 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1733-09-05 at the Kaffeehaus Gottfried Zimmermanns (Collegium Musicum) in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1887 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>Dramma per Musica, For Prince Friedrich Christian's 11th Birthday
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>

<td>45 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices:</i> Wollust [Lust] (soprano), Herkules [Hercules] (alto), Tugend [Virtue] (tenor),<br />Merkur [Mercury] (bass); mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> 1 (or 2) oboes, oboe d’amore, bassoon, 2 corno da caccias (or 2 horns), strings, continuo
</td></tr>
